Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

021250,000044:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021251,000045: 
021252,000046:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021253,000047: 
021254,000048:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021255,000049:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021256,000050: 
021257,000051:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021258,000052: 
021259,000053:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021260,000054:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021261,000055:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021262,000056:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021263,000057: 
021264,000058:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021265,000059: 
021266,000060:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021267,000061: 
021268,000062:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021269,000063: 
021270,000064:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021271,000065:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021272,000066:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021273,000067:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021274,000068:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021275,000069:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021276,000070:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021277,000071:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021278,000072:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021279,000073:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021280,000074: 
021281,000075:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021282,000076: 
021283,000077:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021284,000078:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021285,000079: 
021286,000080:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021287,000081: 
021288,000082:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021289,000083: 
021290,000084:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021291,000085: 
021292,000086:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021293,000087: 
021294,000088:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021295,000089: 
021296,000090:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021297,000091: 
021298,000092:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021299,000093: 
021300,000094:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021301,000095: 
021302,000096:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021303,000097: 
021304,000098: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021305,000099: 
021306,000100: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021307,000101: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021308,000102: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021309,000103: 
021310,000104: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021311,000105: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021312,000106: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20

021719,000513:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021720,000514: 
021721,000515:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021722,000516:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021723,000517:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021724,000518: 
021725,000519:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021726,000520: 
021727,000521:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021728,000522:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021729,000523:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021730,000524:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021731,000525: 
021732,000526:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021733,000527: 
021734,000528:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021735,000529: 
021736,000530:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021737,000531: 
021738,000532:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021739,000533:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021740,000534:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021741,000535:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021742,000536: 
021743,000537:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -

021745,000539:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021746,000540:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021748,000542:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -

022023,000817:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022024,000818:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022025,000819: 
022026,000820:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022027,000821:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022028,000822: 
022029,000823:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022030,000824: 
022031,000825:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022032,000826:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022033,000827: 
022034,000828:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022035,000829: 
022036,000830:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
022037,000831:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
022038,000832: 
022039,000833:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022040,000834: 
022041,000835:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
022042,000836:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
022043,000837:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
022044,000838:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
022045,000839: 
022046,000840:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
022047,000841:                                                                                                  #        
022048,000842:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
022049,000843:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
022050,000844: 
022051,000845:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022052,000846: 
022053,000847:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022054,000848:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
022055,000849:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
022056,000850: 
022057,000851:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022058,000852: 
022059,000853:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
022060,000854: 
022061,000855:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022062,000856: 
022063,000857:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
022064,000858: 
022065,000859:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022066,000860: 
022067,000861:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
022068,000862: 
022069,000863:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

022248,001042:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022249,001043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022250,001044: 
022251,001045:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022252,001046:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022253,001047: 
022254,001048:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022255,001049: 
022256,001050:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022257,001051: 
022258,001052:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022259,001053: 
022260,001054:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022261,001055: 
022262,001056:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022263,001057: 
022264,001058:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022265,001059:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022266,001060: 
022267,001061:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022268,001062: 
022269,001063:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022270,001064:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022271,001065:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
022272,001066: 
022273,001067:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022274,001068: 
022275,001069:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022276,001070: 
022277,001071:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022278,001072: 
022279,001073:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022280,001074: 
022281,001075:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022282,001076: 
022283,001077:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022284,001078: 
022285,001079: 24,3135     1143                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022286,001080: 24,3135                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022287,001081: 24,3135           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022288,001082: 24,3136           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022289,001083: 24,3137           00004                           INHINT                                         
022290,001084: 24,3140           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022291,001085: 24,3141           40140                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022292,001086: 24,3142           00003                           RELINT                                         
022293,001087: 24,3143           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022294,001088: 24,3144           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022295,001089: 24,3145           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
022296,001090: 24,3146           33205                           CAF      OCT205                                
022297,001091: 24,3147           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022298,001092: 24,3150           20623                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
022299,001093: 24,3151           03176                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE
022300,001094: 24,3152           03154                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE
022301,001095: 24,3153           03201                           TC       R23LEM3                               #  ENTER - DO ANOTHER MANUVER
022302,001096: 24,3154           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT

022332,001126:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022333,001127:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022334,001128: 
022335,001129:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022336,001130:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022337,001131: 
022338,001132:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022339,001133: 
022340,001134:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022341,001135:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022342,001136:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022343,001137: 
022344,001138:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022345,001139: 
022346,001140:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022347,001141:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022348,001142:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022349,001143:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022350,001144: 
022351,001145:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022352,001146: 
022353,001147:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022354,001148:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022355,001149:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022356,001150: 
022357,001151:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022358,001152: 
022359,001153:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022360,001154:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022361,001155:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022362,001156: 
022363,001157:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022364,001158: 
022365,001159:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022366,001160: 
022367,001161:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022368,001162: 
022369,001163:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022370,001164: 
022371,001165:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022372,001166: 
022373,001167:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022374,001168: 
022375,001169:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022376,001170: 
022377,001171:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022378,001172: 
022379,001173: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022380,001174: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022381,001175: 24,3206           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022382,001176: 24,3207           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022383,001177: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022384,001178: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022385,001179: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022386,001180: 24,3213           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022387,001181: 24,3214           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022388,001182: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022389,001183: 24,3216           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022390,001184: 24,3217           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022391,001185: 24,3220           33254                           CAF      V16N80                                
022392,001186: 24,3221           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022393,001187: 24,3222           20504                           CADR     PRIODSPR

022396,001190:

022448,001242:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM

022657,001451:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022658,001452: 
022659,001453:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022660,001454: 
022661,001455:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022662,001456:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022663,001457:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022664,001458:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022665,001459:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022666,001460: 
022667,001461:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022668,001462:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022669,001463:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022670,001464:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022671,001465: 
022672,001466:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022673,001467:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022674,001468:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022675,001469:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022676,001470:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022677,001471: 
022678,001472:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022679,001473: 
022680,001474:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022681,001475:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022682,001476: 
022683,001477:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022684,001478: 
022685,001479:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022686,001480:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022687,001481:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022688,001482: 
022689,001483:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022690,001484: 
022691,001485:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022692,001486: 
022693,001487:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022694,001488: 
022695,001489:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022696,001490:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022697,001491: 
022698,001492:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022741,001535:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022742,001536: 
022743,001537:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022744,001538:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022745,001539:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022746,001540:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022747,001541:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022748,001542:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022749,001543:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022750,001544:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022751,001545:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022752,001546:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022753,001547:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022754,001548:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022755,001549:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022756,001550:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022757,001551:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022758,001552:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022759,001553:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022760,001554:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022761,001555:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022762,001556:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022763,001557: 
022764,001558:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022765,001559: 
022766,001560:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022767,001561: 
022768,001562:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022769,001563: 
022770,001564:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022771,001565: 
022772,001566:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022773,001567: 
022774,001568:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
022775,001569: 
022776,001570:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)                                                          ED.
022777,001571:

022813,001607:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022814,001608: 
022815,001609:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022816,001610: 
022817,001611:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022818,001612:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022819,001613:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022820,001614:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022821,001615:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022822,001616:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022823,001617:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022824,001618:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022825,001619:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022826,001620:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022827,001621:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022828,001622:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022829,001623: 
022830,001624:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022831,001625:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022832,001626:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022833,001627: 
022834,001628:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022835,001629: 
022836,001630:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022837,001631: 
022838,001632:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022839,001633: 
022840,001634:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022841,001635:                                                                                                  #        
022842,001636:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022843,001637: 
022844,001638:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022845,001639: 
022846,001640:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022847,001641: 
022848,001642: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022849,001643: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022850,001644: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022851,001645: 
022852,001646: 25,2062  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

022862,001656:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022863,001657: 
022864,001658:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022865,001659:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022866,001660:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022867,001661:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022868,001662:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022869,001663:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022870,001664:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022871,001665:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022872,001666:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022873,001667:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022874,001668:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022875,001669:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022876,001670:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022877,001671:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022878,001672:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022879,001673:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022880,001674: 
022881,001675:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022882,001676: 
022883,001677:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022884,001678: 
022885,001679:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022886,001680: 
022887,001681:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022888,001682: 
022889,001683:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022890,001684: 
022891,001685:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022892,001686: 
022893,001687:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022894,001688: 
022895,001689:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022896,001690: 
022897,001691: 25,2071           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
022898,001692: 25,2072           23315                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
022899,001693: 25,2073           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
022900,001694: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022901,001695: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
022902,001696: 25,2076           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY

022938,001732:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022939,001733: 
022940,001734:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022941,001735: 
022942,001736:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022943,001737:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022944,001738:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022945,001739:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022946,001740:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022947,001741:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022948,001742:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022949,001743:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022950,001744:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022951,001745:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022952,001746:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022953,001747:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022954,001748:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022955,001749:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022956,001750:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022957,001751:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022958,001752:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022959,001753:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022960,001754:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022961,001755:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022962,001756:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022963,001757:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022964,001758: 
022965,001759:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022966,001760: 
022967,001761:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022968,001762:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022969,001763: 
022970,001764:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022971,001765: 
022972,001766:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022973,001767: 
022974,001768:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022975,001769: 
022976,001770:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022977,001771: 
022978,001772:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022979,001773: 
022980,001774:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022981,001775: 
022982,001776:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022983,001777: 
022984,001778:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022985,001779: 
022986,001780: 25,2127           02156        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022987,001781:

023031,001825:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023032,001826: 
023033,001827:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023034,001828:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
023035,001829:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023036,001830:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023037,001831:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023038,001832:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023039,001833:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023040,001834:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023041,001835:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023042,001836:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023043,001837:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023044,001838:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023045,001839:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
023046,001840:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023047,001841:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023048,001842:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
023049,001843:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023050,001844:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023051,001845:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
023052,001846:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023053,001847: 
023054,001848:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023055,001849: 
023056,001850:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023057,001851:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023058,001852:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023059,001853:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
023060,001854: 
023061,001855:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023062,001856: 
023063,001857:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
023064,001858:

023068,001862:

023128,001922:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023129,001923: 
023130,001924:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023131,001925: 
023132,001926:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023133,001927:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023134,001928:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023135,001929:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023136,001930:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023137,001931:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023138,001932:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023139,001933:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023140,001934:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023141,001935:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023142,001936:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023143,001937:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023144,001938:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023145,001939:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023146,001940: 
023147,001941:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023148,001942:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023149,001943:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023150,001944:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023151,001945:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023152,001946: 
023153,001947:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023154,001948: 
023155,001949:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023156,001950:

023158,001952:

023160,001954:

023168,001962:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)

023221,002015:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023222,002016: 
023223,002017:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023224,002018: 
023225,002019:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023226,002020:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023227,002021:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023228,002022:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023229,002023:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023230,002024:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023231,002025:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023232,002026:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023233,002027:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023234,002028:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023235,002029:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023236,002030:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023237,002031:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023238,002032: 
023239,002033:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023240,002034:                                                                                                  #        
023241,002035:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023242,002036:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023331,002125:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023332,002126: 
023333,002127:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023334,002128: 
023335,002129:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023336,002130:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023337,002131:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023338,002132:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023339,002133:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023340,002134:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023341,002135:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023342,002136:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023343,002137:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023344,002138:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023345,002139:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023346,002140:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023347,002141:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023348,002142:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023349,002143:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023350,002144:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023351,002145:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023352,002146:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023353,002147:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023354,002148:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023355,002149:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023356,002150:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023357,002151: 
023358,002152:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023359,002153: 
023360,002154:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023361,002155:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023362,002156:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023363,002157:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023364,002158: 
023365,002159:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023366,002160: 
023367,002161:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023368,002162: 
023369,002163:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023370,002164: 
023371,002165:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023372,002166:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023373,002167: 
023374,002168:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023375,002169: 
023376,002170:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023377,002171: 
023378,002172:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023379,002173: 
023380,002174:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023381,002175:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE - RETURNS
023382,002176:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                         CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023421,002215:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023422,002216: 
023423,002217:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023424,002218:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023425,002219:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023426,002220:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023427,002221:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023428,002222:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023429,002223:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023430,002224:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023431,002225:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023432,002226:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023433,002227:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023434,002228:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023435,002229:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023436,002230:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023437,002231:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023438,002232:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023439,002233:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023440,002234:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023441,002235:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023442,002236:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023443,002237:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023444,002238: 
023445,002239:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023446,002240: 
023447,002241:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023448,002242: 
023449,002243:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023450,002244: 
023451,002245:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023452,002246: 
023453,002247:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023454,002248: 
023455,002249:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR, WAITLIST
023456,002250:

023458,002252: 
023459,002253:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES
023460,002254:
